 kya in donon pakshon ke bich koi baat hui
 In this play, it is tried through Gandhi and Godse and through the circumstances that the dialogue is established that there must be some way out of the dialogue that answers these basic questions
 sahitya ajtak 2019 main shaamil le rahe atithiyon kii list dekhne ke liye yahaan clic karen
 
 
 
 aaj bhi samvaad sthapit karne kii hi jarurat hacharchaa main aage ek sawaal uthaa ki aaj jo saamaajik paristhiti he usamen is ko-aggistension main jahaan gandhi ko maanane vaale bhi hai or godse ko maanane vaale bhi hai, inke bich main samvaad ho rahaa he kya, kya us samvaad kii koi ruparekha ban sakati he, kya samvaad se koi laabh milegaa aapako kya lagata he
 Replying, Asgar Wajahat said, "in my play, Gandhi and Godse speak a dialogue
" pehle main bataa duun ki meraa naatak shuru hota he gandhi ke vadh se lekin gandhi usamen batch jate hai, gandhi kii mrityu nahin hui, ve batch gaye
 He said that i would first like to meet Godse who shot at me
 uske baad gandhi ji ke godse se samvaad hote hai
 Gandhiji says to Godse, look, when you fired at me, some people started hating you, some people started loving you
 prem or ghrinaa ke bich kaa rasta kisi ne nahin khoja or wo bich kaa rasta he samvaad kaa rasta, baatcheet kaa rasta
 He finally said that even today there is a need to establish dialogue because this is not happening
 sahitya ajtak main registration ke liye yahaan clic karen

 main sahishnutaa ke saamaajik paksh par aapako le janaa chahta hum

" satta chaahe jiske paas ho satta samvaad nahin karnaa chaahati, adhikarpurvak badlaav laana chaahati he
 The truth of our country never communicated
 balki apane aadesh chalaate rahe
 It always happened
 isiilie samvaad kii sthiti mushkil se banati he
 The status of the dialog can be made in the public domain
 logon ke bich ban sakati he
 But today people who create dialogue between people are not
 ek samay tha ki hamaare samaaj main aisi shaktiyaan thim

 aaj puri kii puri shakti raajnneeti ko mil gai he

 kala or samskruti kaa hi rasta hamen aage le ja saktaa he

 lekin sahitya or shiksha ko lekar hamaare desh main jaagarukta nahin he

 jab dawa munh main ja hi nahin rahi to vah asar kaise karegi

 rashtriya andolan ke dauraan ham ye jaanate hai ki videshi shaskaon ke haath se sahitya kala or samskruti kaa na sirf vikaas hua balki kai sansthaaen bhi banaai gayi or jaagarukta ai

 aazaadee ke baad logon ke andar se is shakti ko chin liya gaya

 jiske saath samvadaheenata kii shaktiyaan badhati chali gayi

 ye dilli sthit jamiya milia islamia main hindi vibhaag ke adhyaksh rah chuke hai

 ) a strong electoral system strengthens democracy
 loktantric desh main chunaav se sarkaar banati he
 To elect the right government, it is necessary to have maximum voting
 jab matdaan kii baat aati he to paardarshita kaa dhyaan rakhaa jaae, yah bhi bahut jaruri he
 Given this, the electoral process has been transformed
 pehle jahaan ballat paper ke jariye matdaan hota tha
 It has now been replaced by Electronic Voting Machine (EVM)
 iviem laane ke peeche matganana main lagane vaale samay ko kam karne or ballat se bhari mat petiyon ke rakrakhaav main hone vaale kharch ko bachaana bhi tha
 But the transparency of evms also began to be questioned
 jise dekhte hue chunaav ayog voter veriephid paper audit trail (VVPAT) kaa concept lekar aayaa
 Through which the voter gets to know that the candidate for whom he has pressed the button in the EVM has got the vote
 iske liye iviem se VVPAT mashin bhi judi hoti he
 How does VVPAT work? VVPAT machines connect with evms
 jab voter EVM main kisi candidet ke naam or chunaav chinh ke saamne kaa batan dabaata he to VVPAT se ek parchi nikalati he
 It states that the candidate who has voted has got the vote
 vivipat mashin diarect recording electronic voting system (DRE) ke tahat kaam karti he
 The slip appears for 7 seconds
 Which candidate have you voted for? It is seen in the slip coming out of the VVPAT machine
 is parchi main matadaata ko pratyaashee kaa chunaav chinh or naam uski ore se chuni gai bhashaa main dikhaai degaa
 This slip appears for 7 seconds then falls into the sealed box
 kya hota he VVPAT se nikalne vaali parchi kaa?vvpat se nikalne vaali parchi 7 second ke baad mashin main hi gir jaati he
 This machine is fully packed and locked
 agar koi soche ki ye parchi use mil jaaegi to aisa nahin
 Only the polling officer can access this slip of the VVPAT
 counting ke din in parchiyon kaa milan electronic voton se kiya ja saktaa he
 How does the vote and slip match? In case of any dispute in the counting of votes on the day of counting, the votes and slips are matched on the demand of the candidate
 ab sawaal uthta he ki milan kaise hota he? kya ek-ek vot gina jaataa he? to jawaab aasaan he
 The number of votes polled in an EVM is known by pressing the Result button of the machine on the day of counting, which candidate gets how many votes
 isi aadhaar VVPAT kii parchiyon kii ginati kar lee jaati he
 This clears up the situation
 kitne booth par hoga parchiyon kaa milan?isse pehle hue chunaav main har vidhansabha kshetra main sirf 1 booth par parchiyon kaa milan hota tha, lekin 2019 ke loksabhaa chunaav main 21 vipakshi dalon ne yachika daayar kar 50 fisadi iviem or vivipat kaa milan karne kii maang kii thi
 After which the Supreme Court has directed the Election Commission that evms and vvpats should be matched at 5 booths of all the assemblies under Lok Sabha seat
 EVM main kis ummidavaar kaa naam kis number par? jaane kaise hota he taykahaan banati he yah VVPAT vaali mashin?chunavi prakriya ko saral or paardarshee banane or iviem par uthne vaale sawaalon ko lekar supreme court ne centre sarkaar ko nirdesh diya tha
 After which this machine was made in 2013 by Bharat Electronics Limited (BEL) and Electronic Corporation of India Limited (ECIL)
 yahi donon bhartiya companiyaan iviem bhi banaati hai
 It took a hundred years in the idea of VVPAT? america main matadaata ko yah pataa nahin chalata tha ki uskaa diya gaya vot sahi candidet ko gaya he yaa nahin
 In 1897, it was inspected by Horacio Rogers
 jisamen unhone paaya he diarect voting mashin pranali se matadaata ke paas koi pruf nahin rahata tha ki uskaa diya gaya vot kahaan gaya
 The year passed, and the following year, in 1899, Joseph Gray described a mechanism in which a ticket came out of the machine at the time of voting which voters themselves could see before putting it in the ballot box
 haalanki vot ab bhi mashin se hi daale ja rahe the, lekin ek tikat milane kaa saadhan unhone sujhaayaa tha
 The voting machine has improved and reached EVM
 lekin parchi ko lekar ladaai sudhaar kii gunjaaish abhi thi
 Voice was raised by American computer professionals to prevent disturbances in evms by computer security professional Bruce Schneier in the 1990s
 unhone hi vivipat kii demand kii
 In 1992, the American computer scientist Rebecca Mercury reiterated Joseph Gray's idea
 san 2000 main maracuri ne hi maracuri mathed par piechdi kii
 In this, he also gave the idea of a glass wall between the VVPAT and the voter from the machine so that the voters could not take this slip with them
 pehali baar kahaan hua VVPAT kaa istemaal?iskaa istemaal california ke sarcmento shahar main hue chunaav main 2002 main ho chukaa tha
 This VVPAT machine was made by Avante International Technology
 america main 27 rajyon main vivipat kaa istemaal aam chunaavon main hota he jabaki 18 rajya ise sirf local or vidhansabha chunaav main hi apanaate hai
 While there are 5 states that do not adopt VVPAT
 bharat main kab ai vvpat?sabase pehle VVPAT kaa istemaal nagaland ke chunaav main 2013 main hua tha
 The vvpat-fitted evms were used for the Noksen assembly seat in the state in September
 isi saal mizoram kii 40 main se 10 vidhansabha siton par matadaataaon ne vivipat lagi iviem se apane vot daale
 Only 8 in 2014, this time VVPAT was used in only 8 seats out of 543 seats of VVPAT2014 Lok Sabha elections
 ye siten thim lakhanu, gandhinagar, bengaluru dakshin, chennai central, jadavapur, raipur, patna sahib or mizoram
 The commission used 52,000 vvpats in the 2017 state assembly elections held in 2017
 jabaki goa ke vidhansabha chunaav kii sabhi siton par vivipat vaali iviem kaa istemaal hua tha
 In the 2019 Lok Sabha elections, every booth will have a VVPAT machine with evms
 jisamen se chunaav ayog 20625 iviem par lagi vivipat kaa milan karegaa
 Many countries started using banelectronic voting machines on evms in these countries
 lekin security or acurasi ko lekar in mashiinon par sawaal uthne kii vajah se ye waapas ballat paper laut chuke hai
 Netherlands, Italy has been banned in this
 jabaki germany, england or france main kabhi iviem kaa istemaal nahin hua vivipat to dur kii baat he
 Not only this, many states of the country like America have ban on evms without paper trail

 India topped their group and advanced to the semi-finals
 usne oman, maujuuda champion korea or bangladesh par prabhaavshaalee jeet hasil kii he
 On the other hand, Malaysia lost to Pakistan but won major victories over Japan and Chinese Taipei
 timen jab kisi toornament ke semifinal main pahunch jaati hai to unke liye group str kaa pradarshan kuch khaas myne nahin rakhata, kyonki yahaan unhen nae sire se shuruyaat kerani hoti he or jeet hasil karne ke liye sateek ranneeti banani hoti he, kyonki unka saamana apane se majboot yaa phir samatuly tiimon ke saath hona hota he
 At such a stage, the only benefit of good performance at the group level is that the players' morale is enhanced and they are confident in their ability and ability
 yah kisi bhi team ke liye jaruri he
 India will benefit from this, as they have reached the semi-finals by being invincible
 malaysia ko group str par ek haar mili he, lekin is team ne beete paanch-saat saalon main jis str par tarakkee kii he, use dekhte hue pakistan se mili haar uske khilaadiyon kii manodasha ko kuch khaas prabhavit nahin karegi

 america diplomet ne kaha tha ki dalai lamas kaa uttaradhikari tibeti log chunengechin ne is par kadaa aitraaj jataayaa or kaha ki koi anya desh isamen dakhal na dechin ne kaha he ki buddha dharm ke aadhyatmik guru dalai lamas ke agle uttaradhikari ke chayan main uski manjuuri jaruri hogi na ki kisi or desh kii
 China's statement is a befitting reply to the US, stating that Tibet's people and not Beijing will choose the next successor of the exiled Dalai Lama
 'agle dalai lamas ko tibeti chunenge'bataa den, america diplomet sam brownbek ne somvaar ko dharmashala main dalai lamas se mulaakaat kii thi
 In an event after the meeting, he said that the Tibetan people have the right to choose the next successor of the Dalai Lama
 radio free asia (refe) ke hawaale se brownbek ne kaha, 'dalai lamas ke uttaradhikari kaa chayan tibeti buddha system or tibeti netaaon se judaa maamla he
 It has no relation with anyone else nor any government
 'china kii tikhi pratikriya84 saal ke dalai lamas kii tabiyat ko dekhte hue unke uttaradhikari kii talash tej ho gai he
 Since the Tibetan uprising against Chinese rule in 1959, the Dalai Lama has been in exile and is currently in the camp
 china agle dalai lamas ke chayan par apana ekadhikaar jataata rahaa he
 Reacting to Brownback's statement, Chinese Foreign Ministry spokesman Geng Shuang told the media that this was China's internal matter
 shuang ne kaha, dalai lamas raajnneetik nirvaasan main hai jo lambey varshon se dharm kii aad main videshon main china virdohi gatividhiyaan chalaate rahe hai

 China records its opposition to every statement related to it

 In the Tibetan Buddhist system, the Panchen Lama comes in second place after the Dalai Lama
 china ne choki nyima ko hataakar chah saal ke ek bachche benaquen erdini ko panchen lamas chunaa tha jo philhal is pad par virajman he

 dilli sarkaar ne rashtriya rajdhani main prastaavit 3,000 bachapan shiksha kendron ke liye prashikshit karmiyon ko taiyaar karne ke uddeshy se pre-skool shiksha main ek diploma course shuru kiya he
 The course will be started in nine District Education and Training Institutes (dits) from the next academic session
 pehle varsh main 450 siten hongi
 The comments ek adhikarik vijyapti main bataaya gaya he ki sarkaar ne purv main puure dilli main 3000 centaron main bachapan shiksha vikaas kaarykram (isiidi) shuru karne kii ghoshnaa kii thi
 The diploma course in pre-school education aims to build capacity for the ECED program
 course shuru karne kii ghoshnaa karte huye up mukhyamantri manish sisodiya ne kaha ki sarkaar kii 3000 isiidi centaron ko kholane kii yojana kii safalataa ke liye samanaantar rup se maanav sansaadhan kaa nirmaan karnaa mahatvapurn he
